\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a33fdea6f91c5f834105f7415e2a64407}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+QUALIFIER}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__scalar__int__sized_ga22d9cd55823f7c4aeee13aceafd7238a}{int16}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__gtc__bitfield_ga479134317bc95d99f2b2e235d3db287b}{glm::\+bitfield\+Interleave}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__scalar__int__sized_gaf9d6ceaf8a36734c0a026f6f699ff60c}{int8}}}]{x}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__scalar__int__sized_gaf9d6ceaf8a36734c0a026f6f699ff60c}{int8}}}]{y}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Interleaves the bits of x and y. The first bit is the first bit of x followed by the first bit of y. The other bits are interleaved following the previous sequence.

Returns the minimum component-\/wise values of 2 inputs. If one of the two arguments is NaN, the value of the other argument is returned.

\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_addf5ef73283c171730e0bcc11833fa81}\index{glm::gtx@{glm::gtx}!frexp@{frexp}}
\index{frexp@{frexp}!glm::gtx@{glm::gtx}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{frexp()}{frexp()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_addf5ef73283c171730e0bcc11833fa81} 
template$<$typename gen\+Type$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} gen\+Type \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__common_gaddf5ef73283c171730e0bcc11833fa81}{glm::\+frexp}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{gen\+Type}]{x}{, }\item[{int \&}]{exp}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Splits x into a floating-\/point significand in the range \+[0.\+5, 1.\+0) and an integral exponent of two, such that:\+ x = significand \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} exp(2, exponent)

The significand is returned by the function and the exponent is returned in the parameter exp. For a floating-\/point value of zero, the significant and exponent are both zero. For a floating-\/point value that is an infinity or is not a number, the results are undefined.


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em gen\+Type} & Floating-\/point scalar or vector types.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

\href{http://www.opengl.org/registry/doc/GLSLangSpec.4.20.8.pdf}{\texttt{GLSL 4.\+20.\+8 specification, section 8.\+3 Common Functions}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

template$<$typename T$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1mat}{mat}}$<$ 4, 4, T, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a36ed105b07c7746804d7fdc7cc90ff25a9d21ccd8b5a009ec7eb7677befc3bf51}{defaultp}} $>$ \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__matrix__clip__space_gaf2b9bdfe77c910ce3ae07c1a386d110e}{glm::\+frustum}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{T}]{left}{, }\item[{T}]{right}{, }\item[{T}]{bottom}{, }\item[{T}]{top}{, }\item[{T}]{near}{, }\item[{T}]{far}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Creates a frustum matrix with default handedness, using the default handedness and default near and far clip planes definition. To change default handedness use GLM\+\_\+\+FORCE\+\_\+\+LEFT\+\_\+\+HANDED. To change default near and far clip planes definition use GLM\+\_\+\+FORCE\+\_\+\+DEPTH\+\_\+\+ZERO\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+ONE.

(Direct3D clip volume definition) Otherwise, the near and far clip planes correspond to z normalized device coordinates of -\/1 and +1 respectively. (Open\+GL clip volume definition)

Creates a matrix for a symmetric perspective-\/view frustum with far plane at infinite with default handedness.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em fovy} & Specifies the field of view angle, in degrees, in the y direction. Expressed in radians. \\
\hline
{\em aspect} & Specifies the aspect ratio that determines the field of view in the x direction. The aspect ratio is the ratio of x (width) to y (height). \\
\hline
{\em near} & Specifies the distance from the viewer to the near clipping plane (always positive).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\em T} & A floating-\/point scalar type \\

\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_a5b7b33f0eb5a41f3bf47003bbbdc5128}\index{glm::gtx@{glm::gtx}!intBitsToFloat@{intBitsToFloat}}
\index{intBitsToFloat@{intBitsToFloat}!glm::gtx@{glm::gtx}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{intBitsToFloat()}{intBitsToFloat()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_a5b7b33f0eb5a41f3bf47003bbbdc5128} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a33fdea6f91c5f834105f7415e2a64407}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+QUALIFIER}} float \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__common_ga5b7b33f0eb5a41f3bf47003bbbdc5128}{glm::\+int\+Bits\+To\+Float}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{v}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns a floating-\/point value corresponding to a signed integer encoding of a floating-\/point value. If an inf or NaN is passed in, it will not signal, and the resulting floating point value is unspecified. Otherwise, the bit-\/level representation is preserved.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

Returns a value equal to the nearest integer to x. The fraction 0.\+5 will round in a direction chosen by the implementation, presumably the direction that is fastest.

Returns true if x is a denormalized number Numbers whose absolute value is too small to be represented in the normal format are represented in an alternate, denormalized format. This format is less precise but can represent values closer to zero.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_ac3010e0a0c35a1b514540f2fb579c58c} 
template$<$typename gen\+Type$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} gen\+Type \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__common_gac3010e0a0c35a1b514540f2fb579c58c}{glm::\+ldexp}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{gen\+Type const \&}]{x}{, }\item[{int const \&}]{exp}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Builds a floating-\/point number from x and the corresponding integral exponent of two in exp, returning:\+ significand \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} exp(2, exponent)

If this product is too large to be represented in the floating-\/point type, the result is undefined.

template$<$typename gen\+TypeT, typename gen\+TypeU$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a08b807947b47031d3a511f03f89645ad}{GLM\+\_\+\+CONSTEXPR}} gen\+TypeT \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__common_ga6b6e0c7ecb4a5b78f929566355bb7416}{glm::\+mix}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{gen\+TypeT}]{x}{, }\item[{gen\+TypeT}]{y}{, }\item[{gen\+TypeU}]{a}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

If gen\+TypeU is a floating scalar or vector:\+ Returns x \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} (1.\+0 -\/ a) + y \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} a, i.\+e., the linear blend of x and y using the floating-\/point value a. The value for a is not restricted to the range \+[0, 1]\+.

If gen\+TypeU is a boolean scalar or vector:\+ Selects which vector each returned component comes from. For a component of \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{} that is false, the corresponding component of \textquotesingle{}x\textquotesingle{} is returned. For a component of \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{} that is true, the corresponding component of \textquotesingle{}y\textquotesingle{} is returned. Components of \textquotesingle{}x\textquotesingle{} and \textquotesingle{}y\textquotesingle{} that are not selected are allowed to be invalid floating point values and will have no effect on the results. Thus, this provides different functionality than gen\+Type mix(gen\+Type x, gen\+Type y, gen\+Type(a)) where a is a Boolean vector.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\href{http://www.opengl.org/sdk/docs/manglsl/xhtml/mix.xml}{\texttt{GLSL mix man page}} 

\href{http://www.opengl.org/registry/doc/GLSLangSpec.4.20.8.pdf}{\texttt{GLSL 4.\+20.\+8 specification, section 8.\+3 Common Functions}}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}

\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em \doxylink{glad_8h_ac8729153468b5dcf13f971b21d84d4e5}{a}} & Interpolant.\\

\end{DoxyParams}

Creates a matrix for an orthographic parallel viewing volume, using left-\/handed coordinates. If GLM\+\_\+\+FORCE\+\_\+\+DEPTH\+\_\+\+ZERO\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+ONE is defined, the near and far clip planes correspond to z normalized device coordinates of 0 and +1 respectively. (Direct3D clip volume definition) Otherwise, the near and far clip planes correspond to z normalized device coordinates of -\/1 and +1 respectively. (Open\+GL clip volume definition)

\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a33fdea6f91c5f834105f7415e2a64407}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+QUALIFIER}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1detail_1_1outer_product__trait}{detail::\+outer\+Product\+\_\+trait}}$<$ DA, DB, T, Q $>$\doxymbox{\hyperlink{glad_8h_a890efa53b3d7deeeced6f3a0d6653ed3}{::\+type}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a6f7199140605e146e4f573b72e619187}{glm::\+outer\+Product}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1vec}{vec}}$<$ DA, T, Q $>$ const \&}]{c}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1vec}{vec}}$<$ DB, T, Q $>$ const \&}]{r}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_aa916ca426b2bb0343ba17e3753e245c2}\index{glm::gtx@{glm::gtx}!packDouble2x32@{packDouble2x32}}
\index{packDouble2x32@{packDouble2x32}!glm::gtx@{glm::gtx}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{packDouble2x32()}{packDouble2x32()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_aa916ca426b2bb0343ba17e3753e245c2} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} double \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__packing_gaa916ca426b2bb0343ba17e3753e245c2}{glm::\+pack\+Double2x32}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__vector_ga1a8c36c37516ed6f9c13ee66186112ae}{uvec2}} const \&}]{v}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns a double-\/qualifier value obtained by packing the components of v into a 64-\/bit value. If an IEEE 754 Inf or NaN is created, it will not signal, and the resulting floating point value is unspecified. Otherwise, the bit-\/ level representation of v is preserved. The first vector component specifies the 32 least significant bits; the second component specifies the 32 most significant bits.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\href{http://www.opengl.org/sdk/docs/manglsl/xhtml/packDouble2x32.xml}{\texttt{GLSL pack\+Double2x32 man page}} 

\href{http://www.opengl.org/registry/doc/GLSLangSpec.4.20.8.pdf}{\texttt{GLSL 4.\+20.\+8 specification, section 8.\+4 Floating-\/\+Point Pack and Unpack Functions}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_a20f134b07db3a3d3a38efb2617388c92}\index{glm::gtx@{glm::gtx}!packHalf2x16@{packHalf2x16}}
\index{packHalf2x16@{packHalf2x16}!glm::gtx@{glm::gtx}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{packHalf2x16()}{packHalf2x16()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_a20f134b07db3a3d3a38efb2617388c92} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a4fd29415871152bfb5abd588334147c8}{uint}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__packing_ga20f134b07db3a3d3a38efb2617388c92}{glm::\+pack\+Half2x16}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__vector_ga6ebf1ff1f152ff34c800b6997d5f311f}{vec2}} const \&}]{v}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns an unsigned integer obtained by converting the components of a two-\/component floating-\/point vector to the 16-\/bit floating-\/point representation found in the Open\+GL Specification, and then packing these two 16-\/ bit integers into a 32-\/bit unsigned integer. The first vector component specifies the 16 least-\/significant bits of the result; the second component specifies the 16 most-\/significant bits.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\href{http://www.opengl.org/sdk/docs/manglsl/xhtml/packHalf2x16.xml}{\texttt{GLSL pack\+Half2x16 man page}} 

\href{http://www.opengl.org/registry/doc/GLSLangSpec.4.20.8.pdf}{\texttt{GLSL 4.\+20.\+8 specification, section 8.\+4 Floating-\/\+Point Pack and Unpack Functions}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_a977ab172da5494e5ac63e952afacfbe2}\index{glm::gtx@{glm::gtx}!packSnorm2x16@{packSnorm2x16}}
\index{packSnorm2x16@{packSnorm2x16}!glm::gtx@{glm::gtx}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{packSnorm2x16()}{packSnorm2x16()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_a977ab172da5494e5ac63e952afacfbe2} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a4fd29415871152bfb5abd588334147c8}{uint}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__packing_ga977ab172da5494e5ac63e952afacfbe2}{glm::\+pack\+Snorm2x16}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__vector_ga6ebf1ff1f152ff34c800b6997d5f311f}{vec2}} const \&}]{v}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

First, converts each component of the normalized floating-\/point value v into 8-\/ or 16-\/bit integer values. Then, the results are packed into the returned 32-\/bit unsigned integer.

The conversion for component c of v to fixed point is done as follows:\+ pack\+Snorm2x16:\+ round(clamp(v, -\/1, +1) \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} 32767.\+0)

The first component of the vector will be written to the least significant bits of the output; the last component will be written to the most significant bits.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\href{http://www.opengl.org/sdk/docs/manglsl/xhtml/packSnorm2x16.xml}{\texttt{GLSL pack\+Snorm2x16 man page}} 

\href{http://www.opengl.org/registry/doc/GLSLangSpec.4.20.8.pdf}{\texttt{GLSL 4.\+20.\+8 specification, section 8.\+4 Floating-\/\+Point Pack and Unpack Functions}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

Projects x a perpendicular axis of Normal. From GLM\+\_\+\+GTX\+\_\+perpendicular extension. \Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_a9e13be491fd69a438c8fda440cf0156e}\index{glm::gtx@{glm::gtx}!perspective@{perspective}}
\index{perspective@{perspective}!glm::gtx@{glm::gtx}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{perspective()}{perspective()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_a9e13be491fd69a438c8fda440cf0156e} 
template$<$typename T$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1mat}{mat}}$<$ 4, 4, T, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a36ed105b07c7746804d7fdc7cc90ff25a9d21ccd8b5a009ec7eb7677befc3bf51}{defaultp}} $>$ \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__matrix__clip__space_ga9e13be491fd69a438c8fda440cf0156e}{glm::\+perspective}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{T}]{fovy}{, }\item[{T}]{aspect}{, }\item[{T}]{near}{, }\item[{T}]{far}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Creates a matrix for a symmetric perspective-\/view frustum based on the default handedness and default near and far clip planes definition. To change default handedness use GLM\+\_\+\+FORCE\+\_\+\+LEFT\+\_\+\+HANDED. To change default near and far clip planes definition use GLM\+\_\+\+FORCE\+\_\+\+DEPTH\+\_\+\+ZERO\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+ONE.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em fovy} & Specifies the field of view angle in the y direction. Expressed in radians. \\
\hline
{\em aspect} & Specifies the aspect ratio that determines the field of view in the x direction. The aspect ratio is the ratio of x (width) to y (height). \\
\hline
{\em near} & Specifies the distance from the viewer to the near clipping plane (always positive). \\
\hline
{\em far} & Specifies the distance from the viewer to the far clipping plane (always positive).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\em T} & A floating-\/point scalar type \\

\end{DoxyTemplParams}

Builds a perspective projection matrix based on a field of view and the default handedness and default near and far clip planes definition. To change default handedness use GLM\+\_\+\+FORCE\+\_\+\+LEFT\+\_\+\+HANDED. To change default near and far clip planes definition use GLM\+\_\+\+FORCE\+\_\+\+DEPTH\+\_\+\+ZERO\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+ONE.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{perspectiveFovLH()}{perspectiveFovLH()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_af1e5e6d8303f1462e892e0884b66f9fa} 
template$<$typename T$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1mat}{mat}}$<$ 4, 4, T, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a36ed105b07c7746804d7fdc7cc90ff25a9d21ccd8b5a009ec7eb7677befc3bf51}{defaultp}} $>$ \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__matrix__clip__space_gaf1e5e6d8303f1462e892e0884b66f9fa}{glm::\+perspective\+Fov\+LH}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{T}]{fov}{, }\item[{T}]{width}{, }\item[{T}]{height}{, }\item[{T}]{near}{, }\item[{T}]{far}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Builds a left-\/handed perspective projection matrix based on a field of view. If GLM\+\_\+\+FORCE\+\_\+\+DEPTH\+\_\+\+ZERO\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+ONE is defined, the near and far clip planes correspond to z normalized device coordinates of 0 and +1 respectively. (Direct3D clip volume definition) Otherwise, the near and far clip planes correspond to z normalized device coordinates of -\/1 and +1 respectively. (Open\+GL clip volume definition)

{\em far} & Specifies the distance from the viewer to the far clipping plane (always positive).\\

template$<$typename T$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1mat}{mat}}$<$ 4, 4, T, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a36ed105b07c7746804d7fdc7cc90ff25a9d21ccd8b5a009ec7eb7677befc3bf51}{defaultp}} $>$ \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__matrix__clip__space_ga8b7f443c7e30e879fc98fcf1b922d958}{glm::\+perspective\+LH}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{T}]{fovy}{, }\item[{T}]{aspect}{, }\item[{T}]{near}{, }\item[{T}]{far}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Creates a matrix for a left-\/handed, symmetric perspective-\/view frustum. If GLM\+\_\+\+FORCE\+\_\+\+DEPTH\+\_\+\+ZERO\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+ONE is defined, the near and far clip planes correspond to z normalized device coordinates of 0 and +1 respectively. (Direct3D clip volume definition) Otherwise, the near and far clip planes correspond to z normalized device coordinates of -\/1 and +1 respectively. (Open\+GL clip volume definition)


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em fovy} & Specifies the field of view angle, in degrees, in the y direction. Expressed in radians. \\
\hline
{\em aspect} & Specifies the aspect ratio that determines the field of view in the x direction. The aspect ratio is the ratio of x (width) to y (height). \\
\hline
{\em near} & Specifies the distance from the viewer to the near clipping plane (always positive). \\
\hline
{\em far} & Specifies the distance from the viewer to the far clipping plane (always positive).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1mat}{mat}}$<$ 4, 4, T, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a36ed105b07c7746804d7fdc7cc90ff25a9d21ccd8b5a009ec7eb7677befc3bf51}{defaultp}} $>$ \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__matrix__clip__space_ga0786f78f02365fc789c6a4cd809bd441}{glm::\+perspective\+RH}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{T}]{fovy}{, }\item[{T}]{aspect}{, }\item[{T}]{near}{, }\item[{T}]{far}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Creates a matrix for a right-\/handed, symmetric perspective-\/view frustum. If GLM\+\_\+\+FORCE\+\_\+\+DEPTH\+\_\+\+ZERO\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+ONE is defined, the near and far clip planes correspond to z normalized device coordinates of 0 and +1 respectively. (Direct3D clip volume definition) Otherwise, the near and far clip planes correspond to z normalized device coordinates of -\/1 and +1 respectively. (Open\+GL clip volume definition)


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em fovy} & Specifies the field of view angle, in degrees, in the y direction. Expressed in radians. \\
\hline
{\em aspect} & Specifies the aspect ratio that determines the field of view in the x direction. The aspect ratio is the ratio of x (width) to y (height). \\
\hline
{\em near} & Specifies the distance from the viewer to the near clipping plane (always positive). \\
\hline
{\em far} & Specifies the distance from the viewer to the far clipping plane (always positive).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em T} & A floating-\/point scalar type \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_a2b88704e76f42a8894072e73101a56c3} 
template$<$\doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a090a0de2260835bee80e71a702492ed9}{length\+\_\+t}} C, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a090a0de2260835bee80e71a702492ed9}{length\+\_\+t}} R, typename T, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a36ed105b07c7746804d7fdc7cc90ff25}{qualifier}} Q$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a364212a7fa4148cd960bd919442c4fc8}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DISCARD\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{glad_8h_a950fc91edb4504f62f1c577bf4727c29}{void}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__gtx__matrix__factorisation_ga2b88704e76f42a8894072e73101a56c3}{glm::\+qr\+\_\+decompose}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1mat}{mat}}$<$ C, R, T, Q $>$ const \&}]{in}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1mat}{mat}}$<$(C$<$ R ? C :\+R), R, T, Q $>$ \&}]{q}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1mat}{mat}}$<$ C,(C$<$ R ? C :\+R), T, Q $>$ \&}]{r}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Performs QR factorisation of a matrix. Returns 2 matrices, q and r, such that the columns of q are orthonormal and span the same subspace than those of the input matrix, r is an upper triangular matrix, and q\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}r=in. Given an n-\/by-\/m input matrix, q has dimensions min(n,m)-\/by-\/m, and r has dimensions n-\/by-\/min(n,m).

From GLM\+\_\+\+GTX\+\_\+matrix\+\_\+factorisation extension. \Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_af42089d35855695132d217cd902304a0}\index{glm::gtx@{glm::gtx}!quadraticEaseIn@{quadraticEaseIn}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_aa81940d45558cd2ae07fe135e653bcfa} 
template$<$\doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a090a0de2260835bee80e71a702492ed9}{length\+\_\+t}} L, typename T, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a36ed105b07c7746804d7fdc7cc90ff25}{qualifier}} Q$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1vec}{vec}}$<$ L, T, Q $>$ \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__common_gaa81940d45558cd2ae07fe135e653bcfa}{glm::\+round}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1vec}{vec}}$<$ L, T, Q $>$ const \&}]{x}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns a value equal to the nearest integer to x. The fraction 0.\+5 will round in a direction chosen by the implementation, presumably the direction that is fastest. This includes the possibility that round(x) returns the same value as round\+Even(x) for all values of x.


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em L} & Integer between 1 and 4 included that qualify the dimension of the vector \\
\hline
{\em T} & Floating-\/point scalar types \\
\hline
{\em Q} & Value from qualifier enum\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

Returns a value equal to the nearest integer to x. A fractional part of 0.\+5 will round toward the nearest even integer. (Both 3.\+5 and 4.\+5 for x will return 4.\+0.)

template$<$\doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a090a0de2260835bee80e71a702492ed9}{length\+\_\+t}} C, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a090a0de2260835bee80e71a702492ed9}{length\+\_\+t}} R, typename T, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a36ed105b07c7746804d7fdc7cc90ff25}{qualifier}} Q$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a364212a7fa4148cd960bd919442c4fc8}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DISCARD\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{glad_8h_a950fc91edb4504f62f1c577bf4727c29}{void}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__gtx__matrix__factorisation_ga90ce5524aa7390a722817f6c9342e360}{glm::\+rq\+\_\+decompose}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1mat}{mat}}$<$ C, R, T, Q $>$ const \&}]{in}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1mat}{mat}}$<$(C$<$ R ? C :\+R), R, T, Q $>$ \&}]{r}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1mat}{mat}}$<$ C,(C$<$ R ? C :\+R), T, Q $>$ \&}]{q}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Performs RQ factorisation of a matrix. Returns 2 matrices, r and q, such that r is an upper triangular matrix, the rows of q are orthonormal and span the same subspace than those of the input matrix, and r\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}q=in. Note that in the context of RQ factorisation, the diagonal is seen as starting in the lower-\/right corner of the matrix, instead of the usual upper-\/left. Given an n-\/by-\/m input matrix, r has dimensions min(n,m)-\/by-\/m, and q has dimensions n-\/by-\/min(n,m).

From GLM\+\_\+\+GTX\+\_\+matrix\+\_\+factorisation extension. \Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_ace063da94b229a057e3553de18d5847e}\index{glm::gtx@{glm::gtx}!saturation@{saturation}}
\index{saturation@{saturation}!glm::gtx@{glm::gtx}}

Spherical linear interpolation of two quaternions. The interpolation always take the short path and the rotation is performed at constant speed.

\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_a562edf7eca082cc5b7a0aaf180436daf}\index{glm::gtx@{glm::gtx}!smoothstep@{smoothstep}}
\index{smoothstep@{smoothstep}!glm::gtx@{glm::gtx}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{smoothstep()}{smoothstep()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_a562edf7eca082cc5b7a0aaf180436daf} 
template$<$typename gen\+Type$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} gen\+Type \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__common_ga562edf7eca082cc5b7a0aaf180436daf}{glm::\+smoothstep}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{gen\+Type}]{edge0}{, }\item[{gen\+Type}]{edge1}{, }\item[{gen\+Type}]{x}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns 0.\+0 if x \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}= edge0 and 1.\+0 if x \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}= edge1 and performs smooth Hermite interpolation between 0 and 1 when edge0 \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} x \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} edge1. This is useful in cases where you would want a threshold function with a smooth transition. This is equivalent to:\+ gen\+Type t; t = clamp ((x -\/ edge0) /\+ (edge1 -\/ edge0), 0, 1); return t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} (3 -\/ 2 \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} t); Results are undefined if edge0 \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}= edge1.


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em gen\+Type} & Floating-\/point scalar or vector types.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\href{http://www.opengl.org/registry/doc/GLSLangSpec.4.20.8.pdf}{\texttt{GLSL 4.\+20.\+8 specification, section 8.\+3 Common Functions}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_a2824ef6f23df255f86b9c33cebd5da2f}\index{glm::gtx@{glm::gtx}!sortEigenvalues@{sortEigenvalues}}
\index{sortEigenvalues@{sortEigenvalues}!glm::gtx@{glm::gtx}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{sortEigenvalues()}{sortEigenvalues()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_a2824ef6f23df255f86b9c33cebd5da2f} 
template$<$typename T, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a36ed105b07c7746804d7fdc7cc90ff25}{qualifier}} Q$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a364212a7fa4148cd960bd919442c4fc8}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DISCARD\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{glad_8h_a950fc91edb4504f62f1c577bf4727c29}{void}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__gtx__pca_ga2824ef6f23df255f86b9c33cebd5da2f}{glm::\+sort\+Eigenvalues}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1vec}{vec}}$<$ 2, T, Q $>$ \&}]{eigenvalues}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1mat}{mat}}$<$ 2, 2, T, Q $>$ \&}]{eigenvectors}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Assuming the provided covariance matrix {\ttfamily covar\+Mat} is symmetric and real-\/valued, this function find the {\ttfamily D} Eigenvalues of the matrix, and also provides the corresponding Eigenvectors. Note:\+ the data in {\ttfamily out\+Eigenvalues} and {\ttfamily out\+Eigenvectors} are in matching order, i.\+e. {\ttfamily out\+Eigenvector\+[i]\+} is the Eigenvector of the Eigenvalue {\ttfamily out\+Eigenvalue\+[i]\+}. This is a numeric implementation to find the Eigenvalues, using \textquotesingle{}QL decomposition\`{} (variant of QR decomposition:\+ \href{https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/QR_decomposition}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+en.\+wikipedia.\+org/\+wiki/\+\+QR\+\_\+decomposition}}).


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em covar\+Mat} & A symmetric, real-\/valued covariance matrix, e.\+g. computed from compute\+Covariance\+Matrix \\
\hline
\doxymbox{\texttt{out}}  & {\em out\+Eigenvalues} & Vector to receive the found eigenvalues \\
\hline
\doxymbox{\texttt{out}}  & {\em out\+Eigenvectors} & Matrix to receive the found eigenvectors corresponding to the found eigenvalues, as column vectors \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The number of eigenvalues found, usually D if the precondition of the covariance matrix is met. \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}/\+ template$<$length\+\_\+t D, typename T, qualifier Q$>$ GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL unsigned int find\+Eigenvalues\+Sym\+Real ( \doxylink{structglm_1_1mat}{mat$<$\+D, D, T, Q$>$} const\& covar\+Mat, \doxylink{structglm_1_1vec}{vec$<$\+D, T, Q$>$}\& out\+Eigenvalues, \doxylink{structglm_1_1mat}{mat$<$\+D, D, T, Q$>$}\& out\+Eigenvectors );
\end{DoxyReturn}
/\+\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Sorts a group of Eigenvalues\&Eigenvectors, for largest Eigenvalue to smallest Eigenvalue. The data in {\ttfamily out\+Eigenvalues} and {\ttfamily out\+Eigenvectors} are assumed to be matching order, i.\+e. {\ttfamily out\+Eigenvector\+[i]\+} is the Eigenvector of the Eigenvalue {\ttfamily out\+Eigenvalue\+[i]\+}. \Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_a8ab49879d4f64b7b8cca559cf8ff6bb2}\index{glm::gtx@{glm::gtx}!sqrt@{sqrt}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{uintBitsToFloat()}{uintBitsToFloat()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_a774bbb16abffb1644dea6a4cf0f08dac} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a33fdea6f91c5f834105f7415e2a64407}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+QUALIFIER}} float \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__common_ga774bbb16abffb1644dea6a4cf0f08dac}{glm::\+uint\+Bits\+To\+Float}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a4fd29415871152bfb5abd588334147c8}{uint}}}]{v}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns a floating-\/point value corresponding to a unsigned integer encoding of a floating-\/point value. If an inf or NaN is passed in, it will not signal, and the resulting floating point value is unspecified. Otherwise, the bit-\/level representation is preserved.

\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_a5f4296dc5f12f0aa67ac05b8bb322483}\index{glm::gtx@{glm::gtx}!unpackDouble2x32@{unpackDouble2x32}}
\index{unpackDouble2x32@{unpackDouble2x32}!glm::gtx@{glm::gtx}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{unpackDouble2x32()}{unpackDouble2x32()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_a5f4296dc5f12f0aa67ac05b8bb322483} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__vector_ga1a8c36c37516ed6f9c13ee66186112ae}{uvec2}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__packing_ga5f4296dc5f12f0aa67ac05b8bb322483}{glm::\+unpack\+Double2x32}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{double}]{v}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns a two-\/component unsigned integer vector representation of v. The bit-\/level representation of v is preserved. The first component of the vector contains the 32 least significant bits of the double; the second component consists the 32 most significant bits.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\href{http://www.opengl.org/sdk/docs/manglsl/xhtml/unpackDouble2x32.xml}{\texttt{GLSL unpack\+Double2x32 man page}}

\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_af59b52e6b28da9335322c4ae19b5d745}\index{glm::gtx@{glm::gtx}!unpackHalf2x16@{unpackHalf2x16}}
\index{unpackHalf2x16@{unpackHalf2x16}!glm::gtx@{glm::gtx}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{unpackHalf2x16()}{unpackHalf2x16()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_af59b52e6b28da9335322c4ae19b5d745} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__vector_ga6ebf1ff1f152ff34c800b6997d5f311f}{vec2}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__packing_gaf59b52e6b28da9335322c4ae19b5d745}{glm::\+unpack\+Half2x16}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a4fd29415871152bfb5abd588334147c8}{uint}}}]{v}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns a two-\/component floating-\/point vector with components obtained by unpacking a 32-\/bit unsigned integer into a pair of 16-\/bit values, interpreting those values as 16-\/bit floating-\/point numbers according to the Open\+GL Specification, and converting them to 32-\/bit floating-\/point values. The first component of the vector is obtained from the 16 least-\/significant bits of v; the second component is obtained from the 16 most-\/significant bits of v.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\href{http://www.opengl.org/sdk/docs/manglsl/xhtml/unpackHalf2x16.xml}{\texttt{GLSL unpack\+Half2x16 man page}} 

\href{http://www.opengl.org/registry/doc/GLSLangSpec.4.20.8.pdf}{\texttt{GLSL 4.\+20.\+8 specification, section 8.\+4 Floating-\/\+Point Pack and Unpack Functions}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_acd8f8971a3fe28418be0d0fa1f786b38}\index{glm::gtx@{glm::gtx}!unpackSnorm2x16@{unpackSnorm2x16}}
\index{unpackSnorm2x16@{unpackSnorm2x16}!glm::gtx@{glm::gtx}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{unpackSnorm2x16()}{unpackSnorm2x16()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_acd8f8971a3fe28418be0d0fa1f786b38} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__vector_ga6ebf1ff1f152ff34c800b6997d5f311f}{vec2}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__packing_gacd8f8971a3fe28418be0d0fa1f786b38}{glm::\+unpack\+Snorm2x16}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a4fd29415871152bfb5abd588334147c8}{uint}}}]{p}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

First, unpacks a single 32-\/bit unsigned integer p into a pair of 16-\/bit unsigned integers, four 8-\/bit unsigned integers, or four 8-\/bit signed integers. Then, each component is converted to a normalized floating-\/point value to generate the returned two-\/ or four-\/component vector.

The conversion for unpacked fixed-\/point value f to floating point is done as follows:\+ unpack\+Snorm2x16:\+ clamp(f /\+ 32767.\+0, -\/1, +1)

The first component of the returned vector will be extracted from the least significant bits of the input; the last component will be extracted from the most significant bits.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\href{http://www.opengl.org/sdk/docs/manglsl/xhtml/unpackSnorm2x16.xml}{\texttt{GLSL unpack\+Snorm2x16 man page}} 

\href{http://www.opengl.org/registry/doc/GLSLangSpec.4.20.8.pdf}{\texttt{GLSL 4.\+20.\+8 specification, section 8.\+4 Floating-\/\+Point Pack and Unpack Functions}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_a2db488646d48b7c43d3218954523fe82}\index{glm::gtx@{glm::gtx}!unpackSnorm4x8@{unpackSnorm4x8}}
\index{unpackSnorm4x8@{unpackSnorm4x8}!glm::gtx@{glm::gtx}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{unpackSnorm4x8()}{unpackSnorm4x8()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_a2db488646d48b7c43d3218954523fe82} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__vector_ga233f0e8f1aecf686e67c5c39316c4da8}{vec4}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__packing_ga2db488646d48b7c43d3218954523fe82}{glm::\+unpack\+Snorm4x8}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a4fd29415871152bfb5abd588334147c8}{uint}}}]{p}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

First, unpacks a single 32-\/bit unsigned integer p into a pair of 16-\/bit unsigned integers, four 8-\/bit unsigned integers, or four 8-\/bit signed integers. Then, each component is converted to a normalized floating-\/point value to generate the returned two-\/ or four-\/component vector.

The conversion for unpacked fixed-\/point value f to floating point is done as follows:\+ unpack\+Snorm4x8:\+ clamp(f /\+ 127.\+0, -\/1, +1)

The first component of the returned vector will be extracted from the least significant bits of the input; the last component will be extracted from the most significant bits.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\href{http://www.opengl.org/sdk/docs/manglsl/xhtml/unpackSnorm4x8.xml}{\texttt{GLSL unpack\+Snorm4x8 man page}} 

\href{http://www.opengl.org/registry/doc/GLSLangSpec.4.20.8.pdf}{\texttt{GLSL 4.\+20.\+8 specification, section 8.\+4 Floating-\/\+Point Pack and Unpack Functions}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_a1f66188e5d65afeb9ffba1ad971e4007}\index{glm::gtx@{glm::gtx}!unpackUnorm2x16@{unpackUnorm2x16}}
\index{unpackUnorm2x16@{unpackUnorm2x16}!glm::gtx@{glm::gtx}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{unpackUnorm2x16()}{unpackUnorm2x16()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_a1f66188e5d65afeb9ffba1ad971e4007} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__vector_ga6ebf1ff1f152ff34c800b6997d5f311f}{vec2}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__packing_ga1f66188e5d65afeb9ffba1ad971e4007}{glm::\+unpack\+Unorm2x16}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a4fd29415871152bfb5abd588334147c8}{uint}}}]{p}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

First, unpacks a single 32-\/bit unsigned integer p into a pair of 16-\/bit unsigned integers, four 8-\/bit unsigned integers, or four 8-\/bit signed integers. Then, each component is converted to a normalized floating-\/point value to generate the returned two-\/ or four-\/component vector.

The conversion for unpacked fixed-\/point value f to floating point is done as follows:\+ unpack\+Unorm2x16:\+ f /\+ 65535.\+0

The first component of the returned vector will be extracted from the least significant bits of the input; the last component will be extracted from the most significant bits.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

\href{http://www.opengl.org/registry/doc/GLSLangSpec.4.20.8.pdf}{\texttt{GLSL 4.\+20.\+8 specification, section 8.\+4 Floating-\/\+Point Pack and Unpack Functions}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_a7f903259150b67e9466f5f8edffcd197}\index{glm::gtx@{glm::gtx}!unpackUnorm4x8@{unpackUnorm4x8}}
\index{unpackUnorm4x8@{unpackUnorm4x8}!glm::gtx@{glm::gtx}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{unpackUnorm4x8()}{unpackUnorm4x8()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtx_a7f903259150b67e9466f5f8edffcd197} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__vector_ga233f0e8f1aecf686e67c5c39316c4da8}{vec4}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__packing_ga7f903259150b67e9466f5f8edffcd197}{glm::\+unpack\+Unorm4x8}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a4fd29415871152bfb5abd588334147c8}{uint}}}]{p}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

First, unpacks a single 32-\/bit unsigned integer p into a pair of 16-\/bit unsigned integers, four 8-\/bit unsigned integers, or four 8-\/bit signed integers. Then, each component is converted to a normalized floating-\/point value to generate the returned two-\/ or four-\/component vector.

The conversion for unpacked fixed-\/point value f to floating point is done as follows:\+ unpack\+Unorm4x8:\+ f /\+ 255.\+0

The first component of the returned vector will be extracted from the least significant bits of the input; the last component will be extracted from the most significant bits.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\href{http://www.opengl.org/sdk/docs/manglsl/xhtml/unpackUnorm4x8.xml}{\texttt{GLSL unpack\+Unorm4x8 man page}} 

\href{http://www.opengl.org/registry/doc/GLSLangSpec.4.20.8.pdf}{\texttt{GLSL 4.\+20.\+8 specification, section 8.\+4 Floating-\/\+Point Pack and Unpack Functions}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
